    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText17880714576753219099" style="display:none">April 1862. The Civil War has been raging for a year. Union scout James Andrews hatches a bold plan to end the war go behind enemy lines in Georgia, steal a southern locomotive and bring it north, destroying the rail line and splitting the confederacy in two.<br /><br />Union soldier John Wilson volunteers for the mission and embarks on a harrowing journey in enemy country to reach the town of Big Shanty. There, the other soldiers steal the locomotive called "The General" and embark a wild chase through the Georgia countryside with "The General's" engineer, Bill Fuller, in hot pursuit.</span>

<div id="review_3613645789" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3613645789" />
    <a title="MoreTea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/115861627-moretea"><img alt="MoreTea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590491098p2/115861627.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3613645789?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MoreTea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MoreTea" href="/user/show/115861627-moretea">MoreTea</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3613645789" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12764374080319904882">The Georgia Express was a great book for me to read to learn something new about the American Civil War. I'd never heard this story before so took great pleasure in discovering that it is based on true events. The book brings history to life; I was intrigued from the first page to see where the story would go having not known of it before hand. A really engaging book and definitely one to read for anyone that enjoys historical tales. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3610809629" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3610809629" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3610809629?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3610809629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11573870619900441859">‘There was a scrap at a place called Shiloh’ – history becomes a novel<br/><br/>Arizona author Phillip Urlevich was born in California and has followed his love for history and science and crime fiction to his position as a writer. His debut novel was BEYOND EARTH, and he also has written several short stories in addition to the screenplay for SUBURBAN REBELS. Now he concentrates his focus on the history of the Civil War with THE GEORGIA EXPRESS, his second novel. <br/><br/>Obviously a quality scene creator in the </span>
  <span id="freeText11573870619900441859" style="display:none">‘There was a scrap at a place called Shiloh’ – history becomes a novel<br /><br />Arizona author Phillip Urlevich was born in California and has followed his love for history and science and crime fiction to his position as a writer. His debut novel was BEYOND EARTH, and he also has written several short stories in addition to the screenplay for SUBURBAN REBELS. Now he concentrates his focus on the history of the Civil War with THE GEORGIA EXPRESS, his second novel. <br /><br />Obviously a quality scene creator in the cinematic style, Phillip opens his journey back to the 19th century with a setting that ultimately introduces the ‘main character (in many ways) – the “General” - the name assigned to the locomotive of the tale: The year - 1862 ‘The day at the Big Shanty train station started as did most spring Georgia days. Nothing unusual, rather dull. The air was filled with the sounds of the train whistles. Either signaling their arrival or their departure. The crowd swarming and milling about, ushers calling for passengers to board. Were they listening? Probably yes, or possibly no. It would be just another day, albeit a cloudy and rainy one. However, there was only one thing out of place, the large presence of men in grey uniforms wielding rifles, guarding the little train station against foes.’ Having clearly established the atmosphere, Phillip lets the story roll on. <br /><br />The author condenses the plot as follows: ‘April 1862. The Civil War has been raging for a year. Union scout James Andrews hatches a bold plan to end the war go behind enemy lines in Georgia, steal a southern locomotive and bring it north, destroying the rail line and splitting the confederacy in two. Union soldier John Wilson volunteers for the mission and embarks on a harrowing journey in enemy country to reach the town of Big Shanty. There, the other soldiers steal the locomotive called "The General" and embark a wild chase through the Georgia countryside with "The General’s” engineer, Bill Fuller, in hot pursuit.’<br /><br />Relating the Civil War from the Southern point of view makes for a revivifying view of our history. The story flows well, always with the right balance of lightness with the heaviness of the topic. This is a very fine journey to the past. Recommended! </span>
  <a data-text-id="11573870619900441859" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UzMBCzUHYvTLW2/+Bgjnyrbg20rovF9KS5UNNcK8HS41sXnQSd4QoNVoHzcq+NQuQr4IoCz+8OhK1MfNc385oA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Taa96m9GOdVauBFtG6DFwBunMM8BiMah22DTPz0kwqUrJMUxE59LgUSLYaQ3UPYk7/njJcXKaQPaIRnHjOfmKw==')})
  }
